Saɱyutta Nikāya
4. Saḷāyatana Vagga
40. Moggallāna Saɱyutta

Sutta 11

Candano, Suyāma, Santusita, Sunimmita, Vasavatti

Adapted from the 1995 edition of the digital version of the Sri Lanka Buddha Jayanti Tripitaka Series.

 

I

Candano

 

[1][pts] Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāhaɱ pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiɱsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Candano devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto chahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto sattahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto aṭṭhahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Candano devputto asītiyā devatāsahassehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

2.

 

Atha kho Candano devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami.|| ||

Upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaɱ||
Sammā-Sam-Buddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaɱ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāya-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
sāmīci-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho,||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaɱ||
Sammā-Sam-Buddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaɱ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāya-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
sāmīci-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho,||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaɱ||
Sammā-Sam-Buddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||

anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||

Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāya-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
sāmīci-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho,||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāhaɱ pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiɱsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Candano devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.

Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||

4.

 

Atha kho Candano devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami.|| ||

Upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Candano devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaɱ||
Arahaɱ||
Sammā-Sam-Buddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaɱ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāya-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
sāmīci-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho,||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaɱ||
Arahaɱ||
Sammā-Sam-Buddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||

sattā deva-manussānaɱ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||

dibbehi saddehi,||

dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Su-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāya-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
sāmīci-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho,||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||

dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

§

sāmīci-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho,||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

II

Suyāma

 

Atha kho Suyāma devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Suyāma devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Suyāma devputto chahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||

kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

2.

 

Atha kho Suyāma devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami.|| ||

Upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Suyāma devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
Arahaɱ||
Sammā-Sam-Buddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaɱ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāhaɱ pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiɱsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Suyāma devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Suyāma devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjant.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Su-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāya-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
sāmīci-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho,||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

III

Santusita

 

Atha kho Santusita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Santusita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāhaɱ pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiɱsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Santusita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

dibbena āyunā,||

dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Atha kho Santusita devputto sattahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami.|| ||

Upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Santusita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaɱ||
Arahaɱ||
Sammā-Sam-Buddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaɱ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

dibbehi gandhehi,||

dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Iti pi so Bhagavā||
arahaɱ||
Arahaɱ||
Sammā-Sam-Buddho||
vijjā-caraṇa-sampanno||
Sugato||
loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaɱ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo||
sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

Dhamme avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti,|| ||

'Su-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāya-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||

pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

 

IV

Sunimmita

 

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Sunimmita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

 

§

 

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto chahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||

sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

'Svākhyāto Bhagavatā Dhammo sandiṭṭhiko||
akāliko||
ehi passiko||
opanayiko||
paccattaɱ||
veditabbo viññūhī' ti|| ||

sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāhaɱ pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiɱsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Sunimmita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Atha kho Sunimmita devputto asītiyā devatāsahassehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Sunimmita devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Su-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
uju-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāya-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
sāmīci-paṭi-panno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho,||
yad idaɱ cattāri purisa-yugāni||
aṭṭhapurisa-puggalā.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamanaɱ hoti:|| ||

'Akhaṇḍehi||
acchiddehi||
asabalehi||
akammāsehi||
bhujissehi||
viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

Ariya-kantehi sīlehi samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

-◦-

V

Vasavatti

 

Atha kho Vasavatti devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Vasavatti devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho devputto Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

■

"Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti,||
Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

Esa Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho.|| ||

Āhuneyo||
pāhuneyyo||
dakkhiṇeyyo||
añjali-karaṇīyo||
anuttaraɱ puñña-k-khettaɱ lokassā' ti.|| ||

Saŋghe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

viññūppasatthehi;||
aparām-aṭṭhehi samādhi-saŋvattanikehi' ti.|| ||

evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī" ti.|| ||

sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantī.|| ||

3.

 

Atha kho āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno seyyathā pi nāma balavā puriso sammiñjitaɱ vā bāhaɱ pasāreyya pasāritaɱ vā bāhaɱ sammiñjeyya,||
evam eva Jetavane antara-hito devesu Tāvatiɱsesu pātur ahosi.|| ||

Atha kho Vasavatti devputto pañcahi devatāsatehi saddhiɱ yen'āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno ten'upasankami,||
upasankamitvā āyasmantaɱ Mahā Moggallānaɱ abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

Eka-m-antaɱ ṭhitaɱ kho Vasavatti devputto āyasmā Mahā Moggallāno etad avoca:|| ||

"Sādhu kho devputto Buddhaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Buddha saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Dhammaɱ saraṇa-gamanahete kho mārisa Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjanti.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||

-◦-

Sādhu kho mārisa Moggallāna Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamanaɱ hoti.|| ||

Sanghaɱ saraṇa-gamana-hetu kho Moggallāna||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjant.|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||

dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi" ti.|| ||

dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.

loka-vidū||
anuttaro purisa-damma-sārathī||
sattā deva-manussānaɱ||
Buddho||
Bhagavā' ti.|| ||

Buddhe avecca pasādena samannā-gamana-hetu kho devputto||
evam idh'ekacce sattā||
kāyassa bhedā param māraṇā||
sugatiɱ saggaɱ lokaɱ upapajjantti|| ||

Te aññe deve dasahi ṭhānehi adhigaṇhanti:||
dibbena āyunā,||
dibbena vaṇṇena,||
dibbena sukhena,||
dibbena yasena,||
dibbena ādhipateyyena,||
dibbehi rūpehi,||
dibbehi saddehi,||
dibbehi gandhehi,||
dibbehi rasehi,||
dibbehi phoṭṭhabbehi.|| ||
